```mermaid
flowchart TD

    A --> C[Destination Configuration]

    G --> H[Value Files]
    G --> I[Parameters]

    H --> K["values.{environment}.yaml"]
    
    I --> L[atomic: true]
    
    C --> M[Server: kubernetes.default.svc]
    C --> N[Namespace: argocd]
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant AG as ApplicationSet Generator
    participant GR as Git Repository
    participant AC as ArgoCD Controller
    participant K8S as Kubernetes Cluster
    
    AG->>GR: Scan for values.*.yaml
    GR-->>AG: Return matching files
    AG->>AG: Extract environment variable
    AG->>AC: Generate Application manifest
    AC->>GR: Fetch Helm chart
    AC->>K8S: Deploy to argocd namespace
    K8S-->>AC: Deployment status
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class ApplicationSet {
        +String name
        +String namespace
        +Boolean goTemplate
        +Array goTemplateOptions
        +Generator generators
        +Template template
    }
    
    class Generator {
        +String repoURL
        +String revision
        +Array files
    }
    
    class Template {
        +Metadata metadata
        +Spec spec
    }
    
    class Spec {
        +String project
        +Source source
        +Destination destination
        +SyncPolicy syncPolicy
    }
    
    class Source {
        +String path
        +String repoURL
        +String targetRevision
        +Helm helm
    }
    
    class Helm {
        +Array valueFiles
        +Array parameters
    }
    
    ApplicationSet --> Generator
    ApplicationSet --> Template
    Template --> Spec
    Spec --> Source
    Source --> Helm
```
